###############################################################################
#
#/@ (Fi3_xx)
#
##############################################################################

OBJ: Fi3_PLC_Popup_09
   CPAR:
      P0 = Fi3_AStEvMs120
   CFV:  IF S0&3 : Q1; ELSE Q0;
   OPAR:
      P0 = Popup_09
      P1 = Fi3_AStEvMs120
   OFV0:   P0 = ELSE P1;



############ If MB1_PLCLive signal is written but not changed MB1_PLCOK->0 #######
#/@  Communication may be OK but MB1_PLC is not running
#
OBJ: Fi3_MB1_PLCOK
   CPAR:
      P0 = Fi3_MB1_PLCLive
   CFV:   ELSE Q1;
   OPAR:
      P0 = Fi3_MB1_PLCLive
      P1 = Fi3_MB1_PLCOK
   OFV0:   P1 = IF (S0 & 3) == 3 : 1; IF S0 : 0; ELSE;


############ If MB1_PLCLive signal is not changing in 10 s MB1_PLC_CommOK->0 #######
#   Communication with MB1_PLC wrong
#
OBJ: Fi3_MB1_PLC_CommOK
	 CPAR:
                P0 = SysClkSec
         CFV:   IF ((S0 & 3)==3) && ((P0 % 10)== 5) :Q1; ELSE Q0;
	 OPAR:
                P0 = Fi3_MB1_PLCLive
                P1 = Fi3_MB1_PLC_CommOK
                P2 = Fi3_MB1_PLCLivePrev
	 OFV0:   P1 = IF (P0 != P2) : 1;  ELSE 0;
	 OFV1:   P2 = ELSE P0;



############ If MB2_PLCLive signal is written but not changed MB2_PLCOK->0 #######
#/@  Communication may be OK but MB2_PLC is not running
#
OBJ: Fi3_MB2_PLCOK
   CPAR:
      P0 = Fi3_MB2_PLCLive
   CFV:   ELSE Q1;
   OPAR:
      P0 = Fi3_MB2_PLCLive
      P1 = Fi3_MB2_PLCOK
   OFV0:   P1 = IF (S0 & 3) == 3 : 1; IF S0 : 0; ELSE;


############ If MB2_PLCLive signal is not changing in 10 s MB2_PLC_CommOK->0 #######
#   Communication with MB2_PLC wrong
#
OBJ: Fi3_MB2_PLC_CommOK
	 CPAR:
                P0 = SysClkSec
         CFV:   IF ((S0 & 3)==3) && ((P0 % 10)== 5) :Q1; ELSE Q0;
	 OPAR:
                P0 = Fi3_MB2_PLCLive
                P1 = Fi3_MB2_PLC_CommOK
                P2 = Fi3_MB2_PLCLivePrev
	 OFV0:   P1 = IF (P0 != P2) : 1;  ELSE 0;
	 OFV1:   P2 = ELSE P0;



############ MB channel failover #######
#
OBJ: Fi3_MB_FailOver
	 CPAR:
                P0 = SysClkSec
         CFV:   IF ((S0 & 3)==3) && ((P0 % 4)== 1) :Q1; ELSE Q0;
	 OPAR:
                P0 = Fi3_MB_FailOver
                P1 = Fi3_MB1_PLC_CommOK
                P2 = Fi3_MB2_PLC_CommOK
	 OFV0:   P0 = IF P1 && (P0 == -1 || P0 == -2 || P0 == 1) : 1;  IF P2 && (P0 == -1 || P0 == -2 || P0 == 2) : 2;  IF !P1 && (P0 == 1) : -2;  IF !P2 && (P0 == 2) : -1;  ELSE;
	 OFV1:   P0 = IF P0 == 0: 1; ELSE ;



	 
############ Assigning PLCLive from MB[12] #######
#
OBJ: Fi3_MB_PLCLive
	 CPAR:
                P0 = Fi3_MB_FailOver
                P1 = Fi3_MB1_PLCLive
                P2 = Fi3_MB2_PLCLive
         CFV:   IF S0||S1||S2 :Q1; ELSE Q0;
	 OPAR:
                P0 = Fi3_MB_FailOver
                P1 = Fi3_PLCLive
                P2 = Fi3_PLCOK
                P3 = Fi3_PLC_CommOK
                P4 = Fi3_MB1_PLCLive
                P5 = Fi3_MB1_PLCOK
                P6 = Fi3_MB1_PLC_CommOK
                P7 = Fi3_MB2_PLCLive
                P8 = Fi3_MB2_PLCOK
                P9 = Fi3_MB2_PLC_CommOK
	 OFV0:   P1 = IF (P0 == 1 || P0 == -2) : P4; IF (P0 == 2 || P0 == -1) : P7;  ELSE 0;
	 OFV1:   P2 = IF (P0 == 1 || P0 == -2) : P5; IF (P0 == 2 || P0 == -1) : P8;  ELSE 0;
	 OFV2:   P3 = IF (P0 == 1 || P0 == -2) : P6; IF (P0 == 2 || P0 == -1) : P9;  ELSE 0;
	 	 
	 

	 
############ Assigning MB channel[12] Enable #######
#
OBJ: Fi3_MB_Enable
	 CPAR:
                P0 = Fi3_MB_FailOver
                P1 = Fi3_MB_Enable
         CFV:   IF S0||S1 :Q1; ELSE Q0;
	 OPAR:
                P0 = Fi3_MB_FailOver
                P1 = Fi3_MB_Enable
                P2 = Fi3_MB1_Enable
                P3 = Fi3_MB2_Enable
	 OFV0:   P2 = IF P2 != (P1 && (P0 == 1 || P0 == -2)) : (P1 && (P0 == 1 || P0 == -2)); ELSE;
	 OFV1:   P3 = IF P3 != (P1 && (P0 == 2 || P0 == -1)) : (P1 && (P0 == 2 || P0 == -1)); ELSE;

#####################################################################
#
# Change detection signals
#
# If a change signal is written, the trigger is incremented.
# If the MODBUS+ reads the corresponding table, it will be decremented.

OBJ: Fi3_ChangeCount000
    CPAR:
        P0 = Fi3_ChangeS000
        P1 = Fi3_ChDtAck000
    CFV: ELSE Q1;
    OPAR:
        P0 = Fi3_ChangeS000
        P1 = Fi3_ChDtAck000
        P2 = Fi3_ChDtTrg000
    OFV0: P2 = IF S0 && P0 : P2+1;IF S1 && (P2>0) : P2-1; ELSE ;

OBJ: Fi3_ChangeCount001
    CPAR:
        P0 = Fi3_ChangeS001
        P1 = Fi3_ChDtAck001
    CFV: ELSE Q1;

OBJ: Fi3_Analog
    CPAR:
        P0 =  Fi3_PT708_CtWdSet1
        P1 =  Fi3_PT708_CtWdSet2
        P2 =  Fi3_PT708_MinRaw
        P3 =  Fi3_PT708_MaxRaw
        P4 =  Fi3_PT708_MinEU
        P5 =  Fi3_PT708_MaxEU
        P6 =  Fi3_PT708_Raw
    CFV: ELSE Q1;
    OPAR:
        P0  = Fi3_PT708_CtWdSet1
        P1  = Fi3_PT708_CtWdSet2
        P2  = Fi3_PT708_CtWd
        P3  = Fi3_PT708_CtWdSend
        P4  = Fi3_PT708_MinRaw
        P5  = Fi3_PT708_MaxRaw
        P6  = Fi3_PT708_MinEU
        P7  = Fi3_PT708_MaxEU
        P8  = Fi3_PT708_ScaleWid
        P9  = Fi3_PT708_Raw
        P10 = Fi3_PT708_Vl
        P11 = Fi3_PT708_Percent
        P12 = Fi3_ChDtTrg208
        P13 = Fi3_PT708_ValTrig
    OFV0: P3  = IF S0 && (P0 != 0) && (P0 & 1) : P2 | (1 << ((P0 >> 1)-1)) ; ELSE ;
    OFV1: P3  = IF S0 && (P0 != 0) && !(P0 & 1) : P2 & ~(1 << ((P0 >> 1)-1)) ; ELSE ;
    OFV2: P3  = IF S1 && (P1 != 0) && (P1 & 1) : P2 | (1 << ((P1 >> 1)-1)) ; ELSE ;
    OFV3: P3  = IF S1 && (P1 != 0) && !(P1 & 1) : P2 & ~(1 << ((P1 >> 1)-1)) ; ELSE ;
    OFV4: P8  = IF ((S6 | S7) & 03 ) == 3 : ABS(P7-P6); ELSE ;
    OFV5: P10 = IF ((S4 | S5 | S6 | S7 | S9) & 03) == 3 : P6+(P9-P4)*(P7-P6)/(P5-P4); ELSE ;
    OFV6: P11 = IF (S9 & 03) == 3 : (P9-P4)*100/(P5-P4); ELSE ;
    OFV7: P12 = IF ((S4 | S5 | S6 | S7) & 03) == 3 : 1; ELSE ;
    OFV8: P13 = IF ((S4 | S5 | S6 | S7) & 03) == 3 : 1; ELSE ;
